  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_d9cacace-fe88-45b2-ad83-7cba9c0260fb'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer7835405453829341256">The scorching tale of one girl, two brothers and a love triangle…that’s not. Olivia Townsend is nothing special.   <span id="freeText7835405453829341256" style="display:none">The scorching tale of one girl, two brothers and a love triangle…that’s not. Olivia Townsend is nothing special. She’s just a girl working her way through college so she can return home to help her father run his business. She’s determined not to be the second woman in his life to abandon him, even if it means putting her own life on hold. To Olivia, it’s clear what she must do. Plain and simple. Black and white. But clear becomes complicated when she meets Cash and Nash Davenport. They’re brothers. Twins. <br /><br />Cash is everything she’s always wanted in a guy. He’s a dangerous, sexy bad boy who wants her in his bed at any cost. He turns her insides to mush and, with just one kiss, makes her forget why he’s no good for her. Nash is everything she’s ever needed in a guy. He’s successful, responsible and intensely passionate. But he’s taken. Very taken, by none other than Marissa, Liv’s rich, beautiful cousin. That doesn’t stop Olivia from melting every time he looks at her, though. With just one touch, he makes her forget why they can never be together. <br /><br />Black and white turns to shades of gray when Olivia discovers the boys are hiding something, something that should make her run as far and as fast as she can. But it’s too late to run. Olivia’s already involved. And in love. With both of them. Both brothers make her heart tremble. Both brothers set her body on fire. She wants them both. And they want her. How will she ever choose between them?</span>
  <a data-text-id="7835405453829341256" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/422625731?book_show_action=true">Sep 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer422625731" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8222776334359776143"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392492i/755559.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> This seems to be the “it” book of the moment and now I know why! Its a wonderful, addictive read that will have your heart fluttering, have you fanning yourself, with just the right amount of angst and a really cool twist... oh, and twins, REALLY HOT, panty-melting twins :) </b> (see casting pics above and below)<br/><br/><i> <b>“Did you think of my lips when he kissed you?… Do you still want me? Because if you do, I’m all yours.” </b></i>  <br/><br/>Hmmm, I’m getting ahead of myself here…. k, about the panty-melting twins. Olivia </span>
  <span id="freeText8222776334359776143" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392492i/755559.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> This seems to be the “it” book of the moment and now I know why! Its a wonderful, addictive read that will have your heart fluttering, have you fanning yourself, with just the right amount of angst and a really cool twist... oh, and twins, REALLY HOT, panty-melting twins :) </b> (see casting pics above and below)<br><br><i> <b>“Did you think of my lips when he kissed you?… Do you still want me? Because if you do, I’m all yours.” </b></i>  <br><br>Hmmm, I’m getting ahead of myself here…. k, about the panty-melting twins. Olivia is an accounting student who has moved back to her home town to help her now-single dad out on their family farm. The last thing she’s looking for is another bad-boy relationship. But not long after she moves, she meets Cash Davenport, the bike riding, club owning, seriously HOT, tattooed bad boy who wants her in his bed. Like now. He’s <i> “cocky, sexy, charming. Untamed. Rebellious. Heartbreaker.” </i> And despite her resistance to his charms, she can’t help desperately wanting him…<br><br><i> “You’ve never ridden a motorcycle before?”<br>“Nope.”<br>“What kind of bad-boy girlfriend are you?” I ask in mock dismay.<br>“Evidently a terrible one.”<br>I swing onto the bike…<br><b> “Nah, you just haven’t met the right bad-boy.” </b></i>  <br><br>**swoooooon**… but wait! It gets better… The next day, she meets Nash. His twin brother. Yes, twin! As in, identical, GORGEOUS, swoony, and drool-worthy. He’s the good boy, <i> “incredibly handsome, charming obviously intelligent, successful, grounded” </i> – the complete opposite of Cash and the kind of guy she really should be in a relationship with. Unfortunately he’s dating her rich, snobby cousin Marissa who she’s living with, but it doesn’t stop them from being seriously attracted to each other.<br><br><i> <b> “I feel like all of a sudden, my life is a train wreck. And most of the wreckage revolves around two guys. Two guys that, for totally different reasons, are tearing me up inside. Two guys I want. Two guys I can’t have. Two guys I can’t stop thinking about.” </b></i>  <br><br>She wants them both. They both are in her head, in her heart and they both make her crazy for them. And they both want her just as badly.<br><br>Let me start off by saying that I am not a fan of love triangles. I like knowing who ends up with who right off the bat and I’m not fond of characters wavering back and forth but for whatever reason, maybe it was the great writing style, or the drool-worthy characters or what have you, I LOVED it in this book. <b> Completely LOVED IT!!!!! </b><br><br>And you know, the funny thing about love triangle books is that usually, even if I like both guys, I always know which guy I want to end up being “THE” guy. You know?? But, with this book, I absolutely did NOT have a favorite. I wanted them both. Completely. Equally…. <b> Seriously, no joke, I could. NOT. choose!!!!!! </b><br><br><i> “But it’s your rule.”<br>“I’ll break it for you,” he whispers.” </i><br><br>lol, and as usual, best friends really just give the best advice <br><br><i> “Every hen house needs a cock, but only the special hens can handle more than one. Try ‘em out then pick one and stick with it. You’re not old enough to play with two toys at once. That’s cougar territory.” </i><br><br>So… which one does Olivia choose?? You’ll have to read to find out!<br><br>And don’t try and find out in advance… its worth the surprise. There’s a really cool twist! I usually go into books knowing some basic spoilers (like who ends up with who, that kind of thing) and with this one, I went in blind (I was trying to be brave and fearless, its a work in progress) but I am SO SO SO happy I didn’t know. And that’s saying something coming from me. So for those of you who are wondering about it, take my advice and don’t go sniffing about for any details… Just read it!! Enjoy the yummy ride!<br><br>The story sucked me in and had no slow spots. I’ll admit, there was a moment or two that made me squint an eye skeptically at the page and go ‘hmmmmm’, but nothing that pulled me away from the story.<br><br>And about the twist, I’ll say that I didn’t see it coming. I thought it was a possibility, but I dismissed it (silly me!) … If I think too much about it, I’m still not 100% sure how the timelines would all match up and all but its fiction, right? And its hot, sexy, fun, engaging fiction with a story and characters I loved so I’m just not gonna dissect and analyze things too closely. Bottom line, it worked. And I did love the twist. It was perfect for the story.<br><br>Guys, the sex scenes in this book… seriously… I”m not kidding here, H.O.T. Like I think I need to go back and reread some of those scenes… wow! They are definitely adult – this is not a YA or NA read!<br><br>And yes, the book did end on a bit of a cliffhanger… but I was actually totally fine with it. I honestly found it to be more of a lead-in to book 2 than anything – in fact it was very similar to the cliffhanger in Fifty Shades Darker. One where you felt like the main couple was fine, but there were still bad guys out there…. Don’t let it stop you from reading the book.<br><br>But that being said, pleeeeeeease Ms. Leighton, can you please please please release book 2 soon?? *begs* I want MORE!!! <br><br><b> **Edit: just heard from the author that she's hoping to get book 2 out for early 2013. SQUEEE!!! </b><br><br>I highly recommended this book!! Everyone really has to meet the Davenport twins. Go go go!!<br><br>4.5+ stars<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392492i/755560._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="8222776334359776143" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=will-not-continue-series">will-not-continue-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=suspense-or-thriller">suspense-or-thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer430211420" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11170983393780478444"><b>So this book had a few teeny, tiny, flaws.</b> The main character started out as a klutzy (yes, she did trip and fall right off the bat...shocking!), insecure person and said things like, <i>"I'm Olivia, Marissa's slightly dull cousin."</i> I was able to forgive that because she also said this, <i>"I want to paper cut her. On every square inch of her body. And then roll her in salt water."</i> <b>Why, I do believe that Ruthless Bella just kicked Mousy Bella to the curb.</b><br/><br/><b>So I figured out the "twist" before the story w</b></span>
  <span id="freeText11170983393780478444" style="display:none"><b>So this book had a few teeny, tiny, flaws.</b> The main character started out as a klutzy (yes, she did trip and fall right off the bat...shocking!), insecure person and said things like, <i>"I'm Olivia, Marissa's slightly dull cousin."</i> I was able to forgive that because she also said this, <i>"I want to paper cut her. On every square inch of her body. And then roll her in salt water."</i> <b>Why, I do believe that Ruthless Bella just kicked Mousy Bella to the curb.</b><br /><br /><b>So I figured out the "twist" before the story was half over.</b> We're not building rockets here. It's a steamy romance with a very slight element of suspense (which doesn't show up until the end). I just want to be entertained without wanting to throw my reader. This book worked fine for that purpose.<br /><br /><b>So the girl was throwing stones when she lived in a glass house.</b> Yeah, it's not smart to accuse the men in your life of lying when you're the one who can't figure out the difference between man (singular) and men (plural). One is all you need, honey. Unless it's a menage book, which this wasn't. Hot damn, that would have made for a great twin fantasy there.<br /><br /><b>So you got the men mixed up on one dark and stormy night.</b> Well, it might not have been stormy, but it was dark. Why ask who is who? Just go with it, right?<br /><br /><b>So everyone smells the same in this story.</b> Might I suggest a variety of body washes? <br /><br /><b>So your twins are named Cash and Nash.</b> At least it will be easy to redo the monogrammed towels. You'll save money on only having to switch one letter.<br /><br /><b>So this was a short, steamy and entertaining little read.</b> I can't believe this was the same author who wrote <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/395183658" rel="nofollow noopener">a book that made me say FAIL</a>. For all of my little jabs in this review, I enjoyed <i>Down to You</i>. It was the perfect book for the mood I was in. The sex was scrumptious and who doesn't want to get lost for a night in a fantasy of being coveted by two hot, yet different twins? I was liking it.<br /><br />Plus, there is a mention of exploding vaginas. Don't ask, just read. <br /><br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer421463239" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13817409647039635736"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>Nutty bars, zebra cakes, twinkies, fudge pops, twix, reece's peanut butter cups, ding dongs, shots, orgasms, balls, pecs, back dimples, and fingers!! Face it, some of the best things in life come in two's. Even the genius minds over at Wrigley knew...double the flavor, double the fun. Imagine having two...of EVERYTHING! Yes please! <br/><br/>Grab your "oh shit" handle because this book starts off strong! The big "oopsie" moment had me doubled over. Slap my ass in a plaid skirt because I giggled l</span>
  <span id="freeText13817409647039635736" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br /><br />Nutty bars, zebra cakes, twinkies, fudge pops, twix, reece's peanut butter cups, ding dongs, shots, orgasms, balls, pecs, back dimples, and fingers!! Face it, some of the best things in life come in two's. Even the genius minds over at Wrigley knew...double the flavor, double the fun. Imagine having two...of EVERYTHING! Yes please! <br /><br />Grab your "oh shit" handle because this book starts off strong! The big "oopsie" moment had me doubled over. Slap my ass in a plaid skirt because I giggled like a school girl!! I'm also blown away by M. Leighton's ability to juggle three POVs...THREE! Four balls, two penises, and a vagina...and she pulls it off! The flow never faltered...the story kept <i>coming</i>! Amazing!<br /><br />So why not a higher rating? Well, the book was hot (like bend me over the bar hot) and entertaining with a strong plot, but nothing just made it really stand out for me. It <i>would</i> have stood out, but dammit I <i>knew</i>. I didn't want to know, but I knew. From the start, I knew. If I hadn't known, then knowing wouldn't have taken away from the story. I didn't try to know and if I could have de-knowned, I would have. I wish I could take back my know, but I can't. Once you know, you know...and I knew. I really did enjoy the book, but I needed <i>not</i> to know to make it great. You know??<br /><br />Regardless though, I am dying for the sequel. The epilogue left me...well it just left me! It left me hanging, left me craving, left me wanting more!! So much more! You can't just stir up stuff like that then stop. Isn't there some sort of author police out there that can intervene? I NEED MORE!! I <i>will</i> be reading more! Give me more...NOW!!<br /><br /><b>Here's a book random...</b><br /><br />I will never be able to hear this song without thinking of Cash...NEVER!<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=cSnkWzZ7ZAA">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=cSnkWz...</a></span>

It's fair to say my train of thought went hurtling off the tracks and over the edge of a cliff after reading that epilogue.<br/><br/>Unique plot, characters with more depth than the Atlantic and some seriously drool-worthy scenes. mY bRaIn Is dOinG cArtwhEels.<br/><br/>You probably won't believe me, but I had a nice little wordy review lined up for you guys until that bastard of an ending. Now look at me. I'm a freaking mess with my shift key and it's causing horrific levels of erroneous c</span>
  <span id="freeText8645972036915849841" style="display:none"><b>I'll be damned.</b> <br><br>Uh, yeah. It's fair to say my train of thought went hurtling off the tracks and over the edge of a cliff after reading that epilogue.<br><br>Unique plot, characters with more depth than the Atlantic and some seriously drool-worthy scenes. mY bRaIn Is dOinG cArtwhEels.<br><br>You probably won't believe me, but I had a nice little wordy review lined up for you guys until that bastard of an ending. Now look at me. I'm a freaking mess with my shift key and it's causing horrific levels of erroneous capitalisation (Is that a word?).<br><br>So I'm a little slow sometimes (I'm sorry but no amount of coffee in my veins and Red Bull in my system could have made me get even close to guessing the wings this story was about to spout - pun intended). Have no fear, my mouth is still gaping. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451745563ra/17597630.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm actually kind of kicking myself now that I scan the bulk of the reviews only to note that a common point made by most was that they had already guessed the twist <i>halfway through</i>. <br><br>I envy you people with foresight. And a fully functioning brain.<br><br>Clearly I have neither.</span>

<div id="review_442417175" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/442417175" />
    <a title="P.A. Lupton" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5889210-p-a-lupton"><img alt="P.A. Lupton" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442600938p2/5889210.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/442417175?book_show_action=true">Oct 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="P.A. Lupton" class="user" itemprop="url" name="P.A. Lupton" href="/user/show/5889210-p-a-lupton">P.A. Lupton</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer442417175" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1588084577926744393"><br/><br/>I’m not usually a graphic person, but I think this situation warrants it in order to illustrate my feelings.<br/><br/>This is my heart<a href='http://s1189.beta.photobucket.com/user/plupton70/library/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395589i/761966.jpg' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>This was my heart reading Down to You<a href='http://s1189.beta.photobucket.com/user/plupton70/library/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395589ra/761967.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This book had my heart literally racing. I absolutely, unquestionably, wholeheartedly loved it! <br/><br/>First, I need to point out a few things. 1. I LOATHE love triangles. 2. I do not like books written in the present tense 3. I hate cheating boyfriends and 4. I hate cliffhangers. <br/>Down to you has almost all of the above (one point is de</span>
  <span id="freeText1588084577926744393" style="display:none"><br><br>I’m not usually a graphic person, but I think this situation warrants it in order to illustrate my feelings.<br><br>This is my heart<a href="http://s1189.beta.photobucket.com/user/plupton70/library/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395589i/761966.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>This was my heart reading Down to You<a href="http://s1189.beta.photobucket.com/user/plupton70/library/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395589ra/761967.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This book had my heart literally racing. I absolutely, unquestionably, wholeheartedly loved it! <br><br>First, I need to point out a few things. 1. I LOATHE love triangles. 2. I do not like books written in the present tense 3. I hate cheating boyfriends and 4. I hate cliffhangers. <br>Down to you has almost all of the above (one point is debatable) and I still loved it. Does that tell you how good it is that I still gave it 5 stars? <br><br>I don’t want to say too much because I don’t want to ruin it for anyone, but there is a twist I did not see coming. I’d read other people mention a plot twist in their reviews and thought I had it figured out—Not. Even. Close. But because of that twist this book went from great to fan-freaking-tastic! <br><br>It isn’t just that the story sucks you in, it’s the characters. I liked Olivia, but I loved Cash and Nash. It is impossible for you to choose between the two. The author does a fantastic job of writing this triangle in such a way that I didn’t really get angry with any of the characters. That’s usually why I hate triangles so much—I inevitably get pissed off at characters I should like because they make such stupid and selfish decisions. That didn’t happen for me in this story. I’d also like to mention that the cliff hanger in this book is not bad. I hate cliffhangers that leave a storyline unfinished. That’s not the case here. There <i>is</i> a resolution the main plot, the cliff hanger is more an introduction to book 2 which picks up the secondary story arc. It’s not bad at all—well, it left me dying to read the next book, but I was satisfied where this book finished.<br> <br>I know I didn’t really say much in this review that tells you about the book, but I really don’t want to spoil it for anyone. This novel will take you on a ride. It’s awesome, and I recommend it to anyone who loves contemporary romance.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="1588084577926744393" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText3176767890246937904" style="display:none">Spoiler Free Review- Quick Review<br />4 STARS out of 5<br />Genre: Adult Romance <br /><br /><b>Torn between two brothers. Twins. This book will have you <i>wanton</i> and sitting on the edge of your seat up until the very last page.</b><br /><br />Olivia Townsend is a struggling college student just trying to get by. She lives with her rich well to do cousin Marissa. Who by the way cannot stand Olivia she more so tolerates her. None of that matters to Olivia she knows what she has to do and nothing will stop her. She has a plan, helping her dad run his business after she graduates is her agenda. Then one night at a bachelorette party for her best friend at club Duel she meets Cash and her life as she knows it starts to change. <br /><br />Cash owns club Duel. He lives by the beat of his on drum and answers to no one. The second his eyes land on Olivia he knows he wants more. And he decides it's best if he gets more... More of her that is.<br /><br />Nash is the good son. He is currently interning at a top law firm in the city. He's also dating a girl who works at said law firm. His goals are set in place. All he has to do is continue to work towards them, so he does. But after getting to know Olivia he loses focus.<br /><br /><b> They both want her. They both have her.</b><br /><br />Double the pleasure, double the fun these twins will have you<b> hot and bothered</b> by the end of this book. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16001893.Down_to_You" title="Down to You by M. Leighton" rel="nofollow noopener">Down to You</a> is full of sexy witty comments and laugh out loud moments. It has smoking hot sex scenes from anonymous 'who am I' sneak into your bedroom sex, to ride me like a cowgirl on a tractor sex, to O.M.G. scorching-blazing bathroom watch yourself in the mirror sex!! **fans myself to cool off** I loved it! Read it! <br /><br /><u>Fave lines-Scenes</u><br /><br /><i>"So that's how you charm the cobra?"</i> I quip.<br />He smiles devilishly.<i> "If you really want to see what effect you have on my snake, I'd be happy to show you."</i> ~Olivia and Nash<br /><i><br />"How did you find me?"<br />"My brother."<br />"No, I mean how did you know I was here?"<br />"Your father."<br />"You went to my house?"</i><br />She's obviously perturbed by this.<i> "Yes. Is that a problem? Are visitors not welcomed at your secret lair?"</i> ~Olivia and Cash<br /><br /><u>Fave new word</u><br /><b>Deassholization</b><br /><i><br />"No, I don't want you to kick his ass."<br />"You sure? Because I specialize in Deassholization."<br />"Deassholization?"</i> ~Olivia and Cash<br /><br />My Ratings<br />Characters- Lovable and very charming<br />Writing Style- Sexy, Witty and very Clever<br />Plot/Storyline- Savory<br />Steam Factor- High/ Extremely Steamy<br />Overall- I loved it!!! Read it!!!!!<br /><b><br />Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16779859179062966794"><b>Review finally posted<br/><br/>2 stars</b><br/><br/>I'll be honest...I have mixed emotions about this book. I can't quite decide if I liked it or not. The heroine, Olivia, was my main issue. I didn't enjoy the way she played both brothers. Her so-to-speak bed-hopping and her disregard for Nash's relationship with her cousin—even though said cousin was a bitchy ice queen—made her character seem more slutty than endearing. I truly don't believe her character was meant to be viewed that way! Those two aspect, plus the edi</span>
  <span id="freeText16779859179062966794" style="display:none"><b>Review finally posted<br /><br />2 stars</b><br /><br />I'll be honest...I have mixed emotions about this book. I can't quite decide if I liked it or not. The heroine, Olivia, was my main issue. I didn't enjoy the way she played both brothers. Her so-to-speak bed-hopping and her disregard for Nash's relationship with her cousin—even though said cousin was a bitchy ice queen—made her character seem more slutty than endearing. I truly don't believe her character was meant to be viewed that way! Those two aspect, plus the editing issues, pretty much ruined my enjoyment of this book. That said, I can see why many loved this story. It's chock-full of witty, angsty, intriguing, and sexy scenes. Plus, there's Cash! Sexier than-all-get-out Cash! He alone almost made me look past my issues. Almost. </span>

        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer421923333" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8815103741929366734"><b>3.5 Stars...</b> <br/><br/><i>Down to You</i> was a light, fun, sexy book and just what I needed after coming out of an incredibly dark read! <br/><br/>Olivia is a bartender/student who lands a job tending bar for the very sexy Cash Davenport. She is drawn to him and all of his 'bad-boy' qualities way more than she knows she should be. To make matters even hotter, Cash has a twin brother Nash, to whom Olivia finds herself equally attracted. Nash is the epitome of goodness; the type of guy Olivia <i>should</i> be with. Problem there </span>
  <span id="freeText8815103741929366734" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars...</b> <br><br><i>Down to You</i> was a light, fun, sexy book and just what I needed after coming out of an incredibly dark read! <br><br>Olivia is a bartender/student who lands a job tending bar for the very sexy Cash Davenport. She is drawn to him and all of his 'bad-boy' qualities way more than she knows she should be. To make matters even hotter, Cash has a twin brother Nash, to whom Olivia finds herself equally attracted. Nash is the epitome of goodness; the type of guy Olivia <i>should</i> be with. Problem there is, Nash has a girlfriend who just happens to be Olivia's cousin. Quite the devious little soap-opera conundrum, huh? <br><br>There were many elements I loved within this story, and also some I didn't particularly care for. Olivia was a very lovable heroine; she was funny, quick-witted, klutzy, sweet, and very attracted to the sexy Davenport twins. Cash and Nash were hotness multiplied, with a sex appeal that was off-the-charts amazing! I especially loved the way the author handled the transition of all three perspectives; they bled right into one another, with no repeating and no jumping around. It made for an excellent flow and the story was more exciting because of it. <br><br>The story's twist was a little predictable, but I didn't see it coming <i>too</i> early on. Although I felt the characters were very well fleshed out and was connected to them individually, I never really felt a connection with them towards each other, other than a physical one. Luckily, their physical connection was often hot enough to make up for any lack of depth within their relationship.<br><br>Overall, I'd say this book excels in steam. The suspenseful change in tone at the end sort of came out of left field, but it definitely makes me anxious for the sequel. Very entertaining read!<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Contemporary Adult/Romance<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Maximum steam<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Complex and sexy. <br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Entertaining but didnt entirely believe their connection towards each other. <br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> A love triangle with a twist.<br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Decent and engaging,<br><b>▪ POV:</b> 1st Person: 3 Charcater perspective switch.<br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> Yes<br><b>▪	 Next Installment:</b>Follow up. Published and available<br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <span id="freeText1105770039052255205" style="display:none">On my second attempt at reading this book, I am happy to report that I managed to finish it this time. <div id="review_425869138" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/425869138" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/425869138?book_show_action=true">Oct 01, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer425869138" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16173725879708826850"><br/>I love it when I have nothing but fun reading a book and that’s exactly what happened reading Down to You. This book is <b>SEXY</b> and smart, loaded with sexual tension, fun witty banter, and nice HOT spice! There’s enough drama and mystery to keep you turning the pages quickly to see what happens next. I dare you not to have fun reading this!<br/><br/>Cash and Nash are twins, they look exactly alike and are completely hot. There are two! Gosh, when you wear one out, hmm.....<br/><br/>Wait---sorry....got a little distrac</span>
  <span id="freeText16173725879708826850" style="display:none"><br />I love it when I have nothing but fun reading a book and that’s exactly what happened reading Down to You. This book is <b>SEXY</b> and smart, loaded with sexual tension, fun witty banter, and nice HOT spice! There’s enough drama and mystery to keep you turning the pages quickly to see what happens next. I dare you not to have fun reading this!<br /><br />Cash and Nash are twins, they look exactly alike and are completely hot. There are two! Gosh, when you wear one out, hmm.....<br /><br />Wait---sorry....got a little distracted there! <br /><br />So, what I was saying is Cash and Nash are twins who are different in every way except for their attraction to Olivia. How can a girl be attracted to both? Easy. Nash is what she needs: good, responsible, safe, and Cash is what she wants: dangerous, intense, sexy and that usually means heartbreak where Olivia is concerned. But that’s not an entirely true statement either because she’s really attracted to Nash, too and she’s seems to bring out the naughty in him. Unfortunately, he’s dating her cousin who she happens to live with. Right now if you’re like me, you’re backing up and saying: <i>“Ugh! A cheating book?!! Count me out.” </i> That’s what I thought at first too, I hate cheating books! They frustrate me to no end, but trust, no worries. Very little frustration here. I’ll also add that the cousin is a nasty piece of work, I know that doesn’t excuse things, but it did make the situation more tolerable to read about. <br /><br />So Olivia tries to stay away from both, with little success, of course. We are rewarded with the sizzling sexual tension that results. Here’s a snippet to tempt you: <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Decline?" he says, his eyes twinkling mischievously. "What if I insist?" "Insist all you like. My answer won't change." Nash narrows his eyes on me and his lips curve up at the corners. He walks slowly to my window and bends down..."I could always make you." </i>
</b><br /><br />There’s a lot more where that came from. I loved the push and pull, the intense build-up. It makes it oh-so-fun when they finally give in!<br /><br />So if you’re looking for a quick, fun, and flirty read, pick this one up. Do yourself a favor and stay away from spoilery reviews. It’s more fun discovering what this book is all about on your own. <br /><br /> <br /></span>

<div id="review_411639425" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/411639425" />
    <a title="Autumn Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6908049-autumn-review"><img alt="Autumn Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1399327915p2/6908049.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/411639425?book_show_action=true">Sep 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Autumn Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Autumn Review" href="/user/show/6908049-autumn-review">Autumn Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6908049-autumn-review?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6908049-autumn-review?shelf=review">review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6908049-autumn-review?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer411639425" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14195140595024742310">It's rare if I am rendered speechless by a book. I kid you not, for the last quarter of this book, my mouth was hanging open. I mean, I had several different theories of how this story was going to play out. Some were close, some not at all. All I can say is that this book left me stunned, overheated, and wanting MORE!<br/><br/>I'm going to go light on the character analysis, because that is such a huge part of the story. I could truly go on and on and on and on about how much I love Cash, but I'd rather </span>
  <span id="freeText14195140595024742310" style="display:none">It's rare if I am rendered speechless by a book. I kid you not, for the last quarter of this book, my mouth was hanging open. I mean, I had several different theories of how this story was going to play out. Some were close, some not at all. All I can say is that this book left me stunned, overheated, and wanting MORE!<br /><br />I'm going to go light on the character analysis, because that is such a huge part of the story. I could truly go on and on and on and on about how much I love Cash, but I'd rather you meet him. These people have so many secrets and twists that I'm afraid I'll give something away. So, I'm going to do this instead:<br />Olivia-sweet, funny, lovable, hard-working, and determined to succeed<br />Cash-(I literally just sighed WRITING his name) sex on a stick, perfection, sexy, sweet, smart, bad-boy<br />Nash-clean-cut, sweet, charming, responsible, good-boy<br />Ginger-hysterical<br />Marissa-I want to "paper cut her and roll her in salt". Harsh, I know. <br /><br />So, there you have it. LOL Really, I just don't want to say anything more about them. Well, OK I will say this....there are some incredibly steamy, panty dropping, swoon-worthy moments. *wink* <br /><br />On to the storyline. Incredible. Everything you think you will know about it probably won't be right. No joke, I had several theories. Now, I know I've said this before, but I'll say it again...M. Leighton has one of the most creative minds. She brings new ideas to each and every book . I've named her Marvelous M. <br /><br />In a nut shell, I knew I would love this book, but it exceeded my expectations (which were pretty high). There were moments that left me panting (and pants-less-JUST KIDDING), taking freezer breaks, needing to be hosed down, throwing my head in the couch, and in jaw dropping awe. This book will take you on a mind twisting ride for sure!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14195140595024742310" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/424953735?book_show_action=true">Sep 30, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=cover-lust-i-has-it">cover-lust-i-has-it</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer424953735" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9221965427163099567"><br/><b>Sassy, sexy and funny and utterly compelling and engaging – this was a smart, engrossing read.</b><br/><br/>I have to confess that, before I read this book, I’d spotted a few reviews citing an outlandish twist and I did correctly guess what it was so, as I was reading it, I was consumed with the why’s and wherefores’ and watching out for little clues that you may not have noticed if you weren’t in the know. I do agree that this is possibly the most outrageous plot twist since Bobby got out that shower in Dall</span>
  <span id="freeText9221965427163099567" style="display:none"><br><b>Sassy, sexy and funny and utterly compelling and engaging – this was a smart, engrossing read.</b><br><br>I have to confess that, before I read this book, I’d spotted a few reviews citing an outlandish twist and I did correctly guess what it was so, as I was reading it, I was consumed with the why’s and wherefores’ and watching out for little clues that you may not have noticed if you weren’t in the know. I do agree that this is possibly the most outrageous plot twist since Bobby got out that shower in Dallas but I’d have to point out that, in a sea of fairly relentlessly similar erotica, this really does offer something refreshingly different and I enjoyed every second. Despite the crazy plot and the arguably questionable morals of Cash’n’Nash, I read this with a big old goofy grin on my face and just couldn’t put it down. It’s great fun, it’s not taking itself too seriously and nor should the reader and it’s actually a deeply satisfying read.<br><br>So, how would you feel if you started to undress the stripper at your friend’s bachelorette party only to realise he wasn’t actually the stripper but the club manager? Totally humiliated, oui?<br><br>This is our heroine, Olivia who is working her way through college staying with her rich, thin, bony-arsed, obnoxious cousin Marissa. She meets Cash, the aforementioned club owner, and Nash, Cash’s identical twin, legal intern and Marissa’s significant other. She’s wildly attracted to both of them and is completely unable to choose between them! They are both attracted to her and she has the opportunity to be with either one of them.<br><br>It would be easy to judge her for her inability to choose between them and for dallying with their affections but, before you do, consider this – between the two of them they are pretty much her perfect man. Cash fulfils her inherent love of the bad boy, he is sexy, devilishly wicked and completes her need for wild, all-consuming passion. Nash is steady, dependable, loving considerate and she’s also deeply attracted to him and he fulfils her desire for someone a little safer after her disastrous experience with bad boys in the past. Will she go with her resolution to find someone more dependable or will Cash be hot enough to make her forget her convictions?<br><br>So, outrageous plot twist notwithstanding, I really very much enjoyed this book. It grabbed a hold of me right from the very first page and didn’t let go until the final paragraph and then some. M Leighton’s writing style is incredibly moreish and engaging and propels you along as she takes you along a very twisty path and there’s some real laugh out loud moments with her dry, witty style – it’s very hard to put down and I’m delighted to see that there will be a sequel.<br><br>4 stars contemporary romance<br><br>Thought this gif perfectly matched one of the scenes<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Blog</a></i></span>

<div id="review_682822458" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/682822458?book_show_action=true">Jul 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780425269848" href="/book/show/17347631-down-to-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=audiobooks">audiobooks</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3399699-rose?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer682822458" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13307720441622622608"><b>Initial reaction:</b> Yeah...I can't right now. This was not good. I think I'll meditate over it a night before writing a full review, but I don't think it's going to get above a single star.<br/><br/><b>Full review:</b><br/><br/>This is one of those books I don't really want to write a review on, not because I'm being a sloth, or reluctant to share my opinion, but because honestly I really don't want to have to pull this book from my memory and reflect on how...odd this was.<br/><br/>So you guys know about my weakness about reading st</span>
  <span id="freeText13307720441622622608" style="display:none"><b>Initial reaction:</b> Yeah...I can't right now. This was not good. I think I'll meditate over it a night before writing a full review, but I don't think it's going to get above a single star.<br /><br /><b>Full review:</b><br /><br />This is one of those books I don't really want to write a review on, not because I'm being a sloth, or reluctant to share my opinion, but because honestly I really don't want to have to pull this book from my memory and reflect on how...odd this was.<br /><br />So you guys know about my weakness about reading stories about twins - yes, no, maybe so? I was weary because it was a purported love triangle in a New Adult romance, but I figured - whatever, what can go wrong that I haven't already endured to some degree? (Honestly I haven't learned from reading NA yet. *sighs*) <br /><br />Let's first meet the heroine: up and coming businesswoman Olivia. She returns to town to help her father, spends a night at a party with a stripper and finds out that the guy who she thought was the stripper (and she helped take off his shirt) was not a stripper at all, but one of two brothers who seem to sweep her off her feet. Cash and Nash. Nash and Cash. One of them is a up and coming lawyer, the other is the irresponsible, bad boy owner of a night club.<br /><br />Olivia can't make up her mind about which one she likes. And no, she's not fazed by the fact that one of them is currently in a relationship with her cousin because she slams her cousin's relationship with said twin every which way but loose. And then she sleeps with one of the twins and the next morning can't figure out which one she slept with. Dude...how do you...just, gah! That to me is just wrong on all kinds of levels. This is before the twist comes into play.<br /><br />Yeah, I can't even talk about the so called twist because not only did I see it coming a mile away, I had a hard time buying it and the reasons behind it. How can anyone live a double life that extensively without getting caught? I don't understand the appeal of this book at all. The characters were flat, the situations far fetched, the relationships formulaic and the heroine and hero(es) were threadbare. And I'm not surprised that it involved a threadbare mob story because when in doubt, throw the mob as a plot point to make your characters have more stakes. Never mind if it doesn't make much sense or is completely implausible for one man to live two different lives at once without anyone noticing or someone covering up the fact that the second person is actually not alive at all and hasn't been for years. Ugh.<br /><br />Yeah...I couldn't. I'm not invested enough in the characters to follow this series further so best for me to stop here. The audio narration was okay, but unfortunately I don't think it did anything to improve the experience for me in this read.<br /><br />Overall score: 0.5/5 stars</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6747505692188890667">This book is PURE FANTASY!! Twin hotties not only vying for your attention, but also doing it in such a seductive and sexual way that practically every setting of your life leads to foreplay? SIGN ME UP!<br/><br/>The opening scene in Down to You is great...it set the whole tone for the rest of the book. Cash and Nash (but especially Cash...WHO likes bad boys? Me, me!) both somehow pop up in Olivia's life within a day of each other. <br/><br/>Cash is a bar owner bad boy who's sexy, slow smile and flirty ways draw Ol</span>
  <span id="freeText6747505692188890667" style="display:none">This book is PURE FANTASY!! Twin hotties not only vying for your attention, but also doing it in such a seductive and sexual way that practically every setting of your life leads to foreplay? SIGN ME UP!<br /><br />The opening scene in Down to You is great...it set the whole tone for the rest of the book. Cash and Nash (but especially Cash...WHO likes bad boys? Me, me!) both somehow pop up in Olivia's life within a day of each other. <br /><br />Cash is a bar owner bad boy who's sexy, slow smile and flirty ways draw Olivia like a moth to a flame. Though flirt sounds like something a fourth grader does compared to Cash's come-ons. He wants Olivia, and he intends to have her. By 'have her', I mean he wants to F*ck her brains out. But Olivia is done getting her heart broken by bad boys. She knows Cash is the love em and leave em type, and she tries (and fails) to run far, far away.<br /><br />In steps Nash...who's sitting in her kitchen with her beeyotch of a cousin...because they're together. Not only is he the spitting image of the god she met the night before, but HIS interest is pretty clear also. And he soon leaves no doubt that he wants her just as much as his brother, regardless of his girlfriend. Problem is, Nash is what Olivia SHOULD want. He's on his way to being a successful, solid lawyer. He's cool, calm, collected (unless he touches Olivia, then all bets are off.) <br /><br />So Olivia is stuck wanting both boys. What to do, what to do? Well if you're Olivia, you don't have to do anything. These boys are willing to do ALL the work. This is women's fantasy put into words. I loved, loved, loved the first ninety percent of the book<br /><br />Somewhere toward the end, everything sort of comes to a head. Secrets are revealed and all of a sudden, the story takes a huge turn. For me, it was just felt totally out of place. I understand that it was supposed to be a surprise ending, and I was okay with one aspect of it...I'd already kinda figured out the little twist. It wasn't hard. But what is revealed after that just didn't jibe with the feel of the book. Suddenly, it's a romantic suspense? Hmmm...<br /><br />Still, I get what the hype is all about. Cash and Nash are lip smacking good...pure decadent sexual fantasy, and I loved it!!</span>

Perhaps on a 4wheeler, or against a shower wall, or on the hood of the car! <br><br><a href="http://s1303.photobucket.com/albums/ag159/VikaFika/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_m7g7edDPNp1rpvw65.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Olivia, while at a bachelorette, meets Cash at a club through the most delicious way I can think off... By undressing a stranger because of a simple misunderstanding. And what a hot piece to confuse for a stripper!<br><br><i> “If he’s the stripper, then who are you?” <br>“I’m Cash Davenport. I own the club.” </i><br><br>Embarrassed Olivia wakes up to find him in her kitchen, in an apartment she shared with her spoiled cousin. <br><br><a href="http://s1303.photobucket.com/albums/ag159/VikaFika/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_m6eyfhtPIO1qcpx3a.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b> But oh wait... </b> It's Nash, Cash's twin brother who is dating her cousin. She is drawn to them both - Nash is intellectual and a future lawyer and Cash is a delicious, bad boy with layers. Olivia knows what better choice is, from having an awful experience with a bad boy. But her "better" choice is taken... Sigh. OK I am really frustrated with her. No matter how much Cash shows how he is not simply a bad boy, she still stuck in that same experience unwilling to move on and take a chance. I wanted to throttle her because of that. The man spent a weekend doing farm things for her and helping her dad with a broken foot.<br><br>This Love <u> triangle </u> is absolutely perfect.<br><br>There is just enough drama to keep you at the edge of the seat. The sex is hot, the conflicts are just beautiful, and the truth is staggering. I sooooo did not saw IT happening. Will not give more away because you MUST READ THIS!<br><br>Warning: there is a cliffhanger and I am sooo happy I have the next book on my Kindle.<br><br>To sum up:<br><blockquote> <b> CASH!!! </b>
</blockquote><br><i> “You keep looking at me like that and you’re gonna have a big surprise to deal with when you get on this bike,” I tell her.<br>“A big surprise?” she asks, a mischievous smile tugging at the corners of her mouth. <br>“Nah, don’t you mean something more like a Tic Tac?” <br>I love her sense of humor. It’s a little shy, just like her, and it pokes it head out at the most unusual times. I smile and hold out my hand to her. <br>“Then come here and let me freshen your breath.” </i> <br><br><a href="http://s1303.photobucket.com/albums/ag159/VikaFika/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_m83hc1VlzR1r2ogu2o1_500.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

I’m just a little surprised you do.” <br>I can hear the proud smile in her voice. “I saw a special on the Discovery Channel.” <br>“You were watching the Discovery Channel?”<br>“Yes.” <br>“Um, why?” <br>“I lost the remote.” <br>“You lost the remote?” <br>“Yes...” </i><br><br>A Car-less Liv contemplating on who to call to get a ride from, but realizes that she doesn't know WHO to go to for help as she has no idea who she <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ had a nocturnal visit from  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><i> “..There can be no wielding of the Magic Vagina. ” </i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <span id="freeText13237691134482474264" style="display:none"><b>BR with Jo and Sammy!</b><br>(This was a re-read for me)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222858ra/680999.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222858ra/680999.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222858ra/680999.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222858ra/680999.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222858ra/680999.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Olivia Townsend is out with her friends in a VIP room at Duel, a nightclub, for a bachelorette party for Olivia's friend Shawna.<br><br><b>My Olivia</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407905i/797306.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's said that they have a stripper on the way and that Olivia's friend Shawna is supposed to help undress him when he show up. The door opens and in walks an incredibly handsome man and since Shawna refuses to undress the stripper, she opts to have Olivia do it. Olivia can be shy, but when challenged, she can be bold and determined. So when the guy gives her a challenging look, clearly doubtful that Olivia would be bold enough to follow through with stripping him of his clothes, she is determined to prove him wrong and strips his shirt off. Both Olivia and the man who they think is the stripper have a connection right from the beginning. They are both extremely attracted to each other. Even though Olivia isn't the type he's usually attracted to, there is something about her that draws him in. Suddenly another guy walks in and it's soon realized that the man that just walked in is the actual stripper, the man Olivia had been undressing introduces himself as the owner of the Duel, Cash Davenport.<br><br><b>My Cash</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380407905i/797307.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Olivia is mad and embarrassed that Cash would allow her to do that to him when he wasn't the stripper.<br><br><b>"Why did you let me do that? Why didn't you say something or introduce yourself?"<br>He smiles. <i>Smiles,</i> dammit! It registers for a second that it's a stunning smile, but then my humiliation returns and overshadows it completely.<br>"Why would I do that, when letting you undress me was so much more fun?"<br>"Um, because it's completely unprofessional for one thing."<br>"How is that? You ladies ordered a stripper. Does it matter who I send?"<br>"That's not the point. You were being purposely deceptive."<br>He chuckles. <i>Chuckles,</i> dammit! The nerve. "I don't remember agreeing to send you an <i>honest</i> stripper. Just a willing one."<br>I clamp my lips shut. He's infuriating.</b><br><br>Even though Olivia is still infuriated with Cash and what he did, she can't fight the attraction completely.<br><br><b>"You sure are full of fire! Maybe I should've taken <i>your</i> shirt off instead," he says as he pulls his tee over his head.<br>"What difference would that have made?"<br><i>Other than it would have been about ten times more embarrassing.</i><br>He stops and grins at me, a cocky sexy grin that I don't want to be affected by, but can't seem to help myself. That's all it takes to make me forget my anger.<br>I'm staring at him with my mouth open- again- as he tucks his shirt back in. When he's finished, he takes a step closer to me. I stand perfectly still. His grin dies into a seductive curve of his lips that makes my knees feel funny. I'm completely spellbound and embarrassingly turned on when he bends to whisper in my ear.<br>"You'd better close those lips before I'm tempted to kiss them and <i>really</i> give you something to be all hot and bothered about."</b><br><br>Olivia is staying with her bitch of a cousin, Marissa, and if the embarrassment from the night before isn't bad enough, she walks into the kitchen the next morning to find Marissa with a man. When Olivia sees the man he is identical to Cash. Olivia kind of flips out a bit, not quite understanding the situation. The man with Marissa introduces himself as Nash, Cash's twin brother. So she's embarrassed she mad such a scene in front of Nash.<br><br>I don't want to give away anymore of the book, but I will say that Olivia is torn between her feelings for Nash (which he also expresses his attraction for Olivia) and Cash (who has also made his attraction quite clear to Olivia on many occasions).<br><br>Olivia has always been attracted to bad boys and that has caused her <b>a lot</b> of heartache in the past, which is why she sometimes feels that Nash would be better for her. He's going to be a lawyer, he's intelligent, sweet and is Cash's complete opposite. Cash is a motorcycle riding bad boy who is extremely arrogant, and self assured and he is determined to have Olivia.<br><br>This book has steamy sex scenes, lots of deception, lies, heartbreak, and a HUGE twist in Cash and Nash's story that will leave you wanting to read more!<br><br>Cash is by far one of my favorite book boyfriends and this series is by far one of my all time favorites! I can never get enough of this story! This is a book I've read at least a half dozen times because I'm addicted to Cash!<br><br>If you haven't read this book (or the series), I highly recommend you do so- you are missing out on a fantastic series! M. Leighton did a <b>fantastic</b> job with this series and every book leaves you wanting to read more about the story!<br><br><u>
  <b>Some of my favorite quotes from the book</b>
</u><br><br><b>"I grab my purse and keys, sling my overnight bag onto my shoulder and head for the door. I'm thinking to myself that I should've used the bathroom before I left when I look up and see Nash sitting in his sleek black car, talking on the phone. Not watching where I'm going, I forget to step off the curb and end up falling off it instead.<br>I fall ass over teacup into the parking lot. In my head, I envision myself as a comical cartwheel of flailing arms and legs.<br>Yep, I'm making a fool of myself. Again. Right in front of Nash.<br><i>Is there no end to my embarrassment with this guy?</i><br>I'm thinking that as I try to right myself as quickly as possible. Before I can get untangled from my purse and duffel straps, however, strong hands are gripping my arms and hauling me to my feet.<br>I'm face to face with Nash. His dark-chocolate eyes are full of concern and he smells lightly of expensive cologne, something musky. Dark. Sexy.<br>"Are you all right?"<br>I'm discombobulated. "I'm just glad I didn't pee all over myself," I blurt. I see his mouth drop open a tiny bit and I feel my cheeks go up in flames.<br><i>Oh sweet Lord, what did I just say?</i><br>"I am, too."<br>My brain is utterly scrambled.<br>"What?" I ask, dazed and confuse.<br>"I am, too," he repeats.<br>"You are too what?"<br>"I'm glad you didn't pee all over yourself, too."<br><i>Oh yeah. That</i><br>Apparently, it's the rule of the universe that I make an ass of myself at every possible opportunity with this guy. And his brother, too!</b><br><br>~~~~~~~~<br><br><b>"Car won't start?" he asks.<br>"Nope."<br>"What seems to be the problem?"<br>"I have to clue. I have ovaries; therefore I repel all things mechanical."<br>He chuckles.</b><br><br>~~~~~~~~<br><br><b>With his messed up 'do, and his summer-tan skin, he looks like James Bond in his tux. And I fell victim to his charms as if he really were the dashing MI6 agent.<br><i>He's got me shaken and stirred.</i><br>"You belong in a tux, you know that?" He frowns over at me, but smiles. I straighten my head and face the windshield. "Ohmigod, could I <i>be</i> any more random?"<br><i>What has gotten into you?</i><br>He chuckles, "Actually, I think the answer to that is 'yes'."<br>"You know me well, Bond."<br>He chuckles again. "Bond? As in James Bond? Where did that come from?"<br>I turn my head to look at him again. Immediately it gets all fuzzy with hormones.<br>"Um, I was, uh, I was thinking about being shaken and stirred." He looks over at me and quirks one brow. "I mean I was thinking how well you could probably shake and stir something."<br><i>Ohmigod, somebody stop me!</i><br>"I mean, how well you could probably shake and stir a drink. Not me." I snort.<br><i>Ohmigod, I just snorted!"</i><br>"You were?" His mouth curves into a sexy grin. With the brow raised and those lips curled up at the corners, he looks exactly like his brother. Like the twins that they are.</b><br><br>~~~~~~~~<br><br><b>
  <i>Note to self: Do not expect coherent thought to be possible when staring at Nash. Motor skills may be impaired as well. Take necessary precautions.<br>I almost snicker when I picture myself putting on a helmet, knee pads and a mouth guard every time Nash enters a room.<br>Then I think of what I could do in the knee pads....</i>
</b><br><br>~~~~~~~~<br><br><b>"Uh-huh. This sounds like penis problems."<br>"Ohmigod, Ginger! It's not penis problems. You think everything is about sex."<br>"Isn't it?"<br>I laugh. "No. It's not."<br>"So this has nothing to do with a guy?"<br>I pause.<br>"Ah-ha! I knew it! Penis problems."<br>"Well, it seems that the <i>cause</i> of some of my problems happens to <i>have</i> a penis. Well, two actually."<br>"Oh sweet Mary! You're dating a guy with two dicks?"<br>"Ginger, no! It's about two different guys."<br>"Oh," she says, obviously disappointed. "Damn. That woulda been kinda cool."<br>"How so?"<br>"I don't know. One for each hole?"<br>"You're sick, you know that?"<br>"Yeah, pretty much"<br>I laugh again. "At least you're not afraid to admit it."</b><br><br>~~~~~~~~<br><br><b>"In the meantime, get those penis problems fixed. Every hen house needs a cock, but only the special hens can handle more than one. Try 'em out then pick one and stick with it. You're not old enough to play with two toys at the same time. That's cougar territory."<br>"I'll try to remember that," I say derisively.</b><br><br>~~~~~~~~<br><br><b>His eyes narrow on me, but again he says nothing.<br>He's a very perceptive guy.<br>"And this bad-boy boyfriend?"<br>"Bad boy?"<br>"Yeah. The type you apparently avoid now."<br>"Oh, right." I laugh. It's a single bark of bitterness. "Ummm, he fell into a wood chipper?" I ask, hoping he'll get the hint that I don't really want to talk about him either.<br>He pauses with his drink halfway to his mouth, as if judging whether or not I'm serious, then he grins and takes a sip.<br>"Poor guy. And the one before that?"<br>"Eaten by a shark?"<br>"And before that?"<br>"Kidnapped by a travelling circus?"<br>He chuckles. "Wow. Your life's like a cautionary tale."<br>"Future suitors be warned."<br>"I'm willing to take my chances," he says with a wink.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380222858i/681003.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></b></span>

  <span id="freeText3488088091383090175" style="display:none">This book is super addictive and hard to put down. Olivia finds herself in a quandary when she meets a guy she’s instantly attracted to, but won’t be dating because she’s done with bad boys, and then discovers her cousin is dating his twin, who seems to have the hots for her as well. Nash and Cash look the same but are night and day in personality, and Olivia has personal issues from her past leaving her torn between what is right for her. <br /><br />This is one of those scenarios that’s tricky to get right, someone torn between brothers, and here, it works. Plus, there are twists and turns and revelations along the way that are quite shocking! A quick, exciting read! <br /><br />Please excuse typos/name misspellings. <span id="freeTextContainer12313115128717391522">Olivia's in college working her way towards an accounting degree and working at a bar when she meets Cash, a club owner and obvious bad boy. There is an immediate attraction but she has sworn off bad boys. Imagine her surprise when she meets her cousin's boyfriend, Nash...that's right, Cash's twin....and the good boy but he's taken...or is he? <br/><br/>I think I smiled through this whole book...well, except maybe the Gollumesque epilogue. I loved the banter...the flirting and teasing that went on between</span>
  <span id="freeText12313115128717391522" style="display:none">Olivia's in college working her way towards an accounting degree and working at a bar when she meets Cash, a club owner and obvious bad boy. There is an immediate attraction but she has sworn off bad boys. Imagine her surprise when she meets her cousin's boyfriend, Nash...that's right, Cash's twin....and the good boy but he's taken...or is he? <br /><br />I think I smiled through this whole book...well, except maybe the Gollumesque epilogue. I loved the banter...the flirting and teasing that went on between Olivia and Cash and Olivia and Nash. You can definitely see how conflicted Olivia can be with both men being great in their own ways. <br /><br />I really enjoyed Olivia...she's so feisty and I laughed at some of the things that she said. I loved her wanting to be a good person and trying not to fall back on bad patterns. Too bad she just can't help herself.<br /><br />I love both Cash and Nash. I really don't think I could pick one...well, maybe. (Cash!!) ;) They both have great qualities and phewww some steamy sex scenes. I also LOVED having all the different POV's. It was great knowing what everyone thought!<br /><br />There's some interesting secondary characters. I loved Olivia's Dad and Ginger is a hoot! I can't wait to see how things are with Marissa in the next book.<br /><br />One of the things that bothered me was the use of "Ohmigod" and "effin". While it wasn't used a huge amount of times, it just felt like it was and I couldn't help but roll my eyes each time! <br /><br />Okay...so there's a big plot twist and yes, I wondered if it would go that way. I almost wished it hadn't. I really enjoyed the two brothers and wondering who Olivia would go with. But...I'm enjoying the twist as well. <br /><br />I do have to say that it's unfinished. There's some drama with Cash and Nash having a secret. And I eluded to the "Gollumesque" epilogue with a really creepy individual named Duffy that reminds me of Gollum from <i>Lords of the Rings</i>. He's really freaky! <br /><br />But 'm really looking forward to the "To Be Continued." This book was nice...getting to know everyone and finding out the secret but I'm hoping the next book will have more substance. I look forward to Olivia's relationship with "whoever" and how things will work out.<br /><br /><br />Favorite quotes:<br /><br />♦ "If there’s one thing I’ve got, it’s junk in my trunk."<br /><br />♥ “I shouldn't have stayed as long as I did, but I wanted to hold her while she slept. I wanted her to know I wasn't going anywhere. That she was safe with me. In my arms.”<br /></span>

We undress each other as though we’ve never made love, as though this is the first time and we can’t wait one more second to feel skin on skin.<br/>When he enters me , my whole world collapses . It melts and covers us as he moves within me , like a perfect crystalline cocoon . </i>
</b><br/><br/>Michelle Leighton rocks the adult contemporary scene with her first adult romance read !!! Phew , the lady definitely can writ</span>
  <span id="freeText6844122054187979377" style="display:none"><b>
  <i> His hands are hungry and urgent as he grabs me around the waist and turns to lay me on the bed. We undress each other as though we’ve never made love, as though this is the first time and we can’t wait one more second to feel skin on skin.<br>When he enters me , my whole world collapses . It melts and covers us as he moves within me , like a perfect crystalline cocoon . </i>
</b><br><br>Michelle Leighton rocks the adult contemporary scene with her first adult romance read !!! Phew , the lady definitely can write up some pretty hot stuff with two uber hot and handsome male leads and one not so shy female lead !!<br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/eye%20wink/millionsofgifs/tumblr_lly7g4q1nj1qzoaqio1_400.gif?o=36" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392228ra/755123.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Cue <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=IkdTBlI0c3U" rel="nofollow noopener"> Beautiful Dangerous - Slash ft. Fergie </a><br><br>Olivia Townsend is a girl trying to live her life plain and simple with no distractions what so ever . She just wants to get done with her college and go back to taking care of her dad and their farm . But what she isn't prepared for is the different forms of distractions that are going to turn her life upside down . Distraction 1 code name Cash Davenport ,the owner of a club and your typical yet not so typical bad boy . He is a hot , cocky , blessed with a devilish grin motherfreaker . The kind of boy you wouldn't want your mom to meet . He is what Olivia craves or should I say is attracted to . He is the kind of guy she has promised herself to stir clear of . But she cant really help herself can she ?? Typical lady like always falling for the bad boys ! Enters Distraction 2 code name Nash Davenport , Cash's twin brother . Nash is everything Cash isn't . He is highly respected , working as a intern at a law firm and is engaged to the daughter of one of the head of the law firm . He is what Olivia needs , a guy who is intelligent , good and respectable . But there's a problem , he's already engaged to Marissa , Olivia's snobby cousin . But what if both these hottie's want Olivia . And then there's a secret too ! What is that secret ? Who will Olivia choose ?? Answers to all those questions will only be revealed if you manage to get the book and read it . <br><br>Like I said earlier Michelle really proves her mettle here by writing a story that is not YA . And let me add that she does it absolute panache . The story is intriguing . Its told from alternate POV's constantly switching from Olivia to Cash to Nash . I love stories told from alternate POV's as they give readers more access to the character mindsets . Another thing that really was gnawing on me was , ' A love triangle , that isn't ' mentioned in the blurb . And I might have to say this proudly , I figured that out even before I started reading the story !!!! Aha, ain't I one smart pants !! ;P <br><br>The mystery part of the book is interesting as well . As a matter of fact , that part is just getting started . Yes, this book most certainly has a sequel and the danger of the secrets that were revealed in this book will start clawing their way to our characters in the next book for sure . The characters were enjoyable and the sex was hot like really hot ! Oh I need a fan here ! <br><br>All in all , a fantastically written story with some really hot humor , some hot mystery and some more hotness added in by its characters ! This one's a hot must read !!! </span>
