<span id="freeTextContainer15369380709118476336"><b>
  <i>“OHMIGOD, HE WAS SO EFFIN’ HOT!”</i>
</b><br/><br/>I can’t even remember who this quote was about, but it totally didn’t matter because this book has two AMAZING hotties! <br/><br/>Bad boy Cash – <i>“Cocky, sexy, charming. Untamed. Rebellious. Heartbreaker”</i><br/><br/>And his twin brother, the ‘good boy’ Nash – <i>“Incredibly handsome, charming, obviously intelligent, successful, grounded, responsible" </i><br/><br/>Torn between these two gorgeous heroes (not a bad place to be, really!) is our heroine, Olivia - a regular girl (although super hot and d</span>
  <span id="freeText15369380709118476336" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“OHMIGOD, HE WAS SO EFFIN’ HOT!”</i>
</b><br /><br />I can’t even remember who this quote was about, but it totally didn’t matter because this book has two AMAZING hotties! <br /><br />Bad boy Cash – <i>“Cocky, sexy, charming. Untamed. Rebellious. Heartbreaker”</i><br /><br />And his twin brother, the ‘good boy’ Nash – <i>“Incredibly handsome, charming, obviously intelligent, successful, grounded, responsible" </i><br /><br />Torn between these two gorgeous heroes (not a bad place to be, really!) is our heroine, Olivia - a regular girl (although super hot and devastatingly sexy) with a history of having her heart broken by bad boys. She meets Cash on page 2 and hot damn! Instant chemistry! However, in an effort to protect herself from future hurt, although she is dangerously attracted to Cash, she tries to ignore the way she feels about him. She then meets his identical twin brother, Nash, who is exactly the kind of guy she should be with, and also definitely gets her panties is a twist. However, Nash, is already involved with her bitch of a cousin.<br /><br />This sets up the love triangle that is this book, and I freaking loved it! Olivia tries hard to resist both brothers, even though she wants them… badly! I don’t want to give too much away so won’t say much more than that, but damn, this book is just sizzling with chemistry! There is so much hotness going on in this book, I think I actually shivered a couple of times with all of the sexy banter and shenanigans that were going on!<br /><br /><i>"His eyes meet mine and one brow rises in that </i>holy mother of hell<i> – sexy way, then he mutters, "You’ve got one chance to make my mouth water."<br />I suck in a breath. And chills break out down my arms. </i><br />Damn, he’s good!"<br /><br />Told from mixed POVs from all three of the main characters we get to see the attraction building from the very start, and the sexual tension is full-on, providing lots of laughs, heaps of squee moments, and some serious steam (wow, those scenes are smoking hot!!!). And once an actual love story starts to develop, it is absolutely gorgeous! Sooooo incredibly swoony, and so beautifully written, I could feel the emotion - it’s almost embarrassing to admit but at one point I actually had goosebumps! <br /><br /><i>“Shhh, just let me love you, okay? Don't think. Just feel.”</i><br /><br />And this…<br /><br /><i>“I shouldn't have stayed as long as I did, but I wanted to hold her while she slept. I wanted her to know I wasn't going anywhere. That she was safe with me. In my arms.”</i><br /><br />SWOOOOOOOOOOON!!!<br /><br />There are also some really funny moments, and I have to give a shout out to Olivia’s friend Ginger, who had me in hysterics whenever she showed up. <br /><br /><i>“Ah-ha! I knew it! Penis problems”<br />“Well, it seems that the cause of some of my problems happens to have a penis. Well, two actually,”<br />“Oh sweet Mary! You’re dating a guy with two dicks?”<br />“Ginger, no! It’s about two different guys.”<br />“Oh,” she says, obviously disappointed. “Damn. That woulda been kinda cool.”</i><br /><br />I really loved this book. It’s funny, it’s romantic, it’s hot but there’s also some drama, and a few surprises thrown in along the way (although I picked the main one pretty early on in the story). The epilogue sort of came out of nowhere, but leads in nicely to book 2. <br /><br />Looking forward to seeing more of these gorgeous characters!<br /><br />4.5 stars :)</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer420439479" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10407886818811187341">This one has a pretty ridiculous and outlandish major plot twist, but it also has a lot of *damn* funny lines. The humor's not OTT (like a certain book I could mention that's gotten a lot of buzz in recent months). It's smart, well-placed humor. That was one of my very favorite things about this book. And, I have to say, outlandish plot twist or not, I read and enjoyed the whole darn book! It's a funny, steamy, light read. And, as the author warns, it is not YA or even New Adult. It truly is an </span>
  <span id="freeText10407886818811187341" style="display:none">This one has a pretty ridiculous and outlandish major plot twist, but it also has a lot of *damn* funny lines. The humor's not OTT (like a certain book I could mention that's gotten a lot of buzz in recent months). It's smart, well-placed humor. That was one of my very favorite things about this book. And, I have to say, outlandish plot twist or not, I read and enjoyed the whole darn book! It's a funny, steamy, light read. And, as the author warns, it is not YA or even New Adult. It truly is an adult contemporary romance. Give it a try!</span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_416795946" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/416795946" />
    <a title="Erin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4979538-erin"><img alt="Erin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1520654483p2/4979538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/416795946?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Erin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Erin" href="/user/show/4979538-erin">Erin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4979538-erin?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4979538-erin?shelf=romance-erotica-faves">romance-erotica-faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4979538-erin?shelf=autographed-books">autographed-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer416795946" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10820911726280864072">GAH! I didn't know this story was more than one book, how can it end like that??!! *takes deep breath* My dear Ms. Leighton, you are trying to torture us, but at least you gave us quite the treat first with this hot number that had my pulse racing!!<br/><br/>I was so excited to get my hands on this book when I first read about it, and Leighton seems to get better every time so I was expecting great things. In Down to You, Olivia is just your average girl with the typical financial woes that college studen</span>
  <span id="freeText10820911726280864072" style="display:none">GAH! I didn't know this story was more than one book, how can it end like that??!! *takes deep breath* My dear Ms. Leighton, you are trying to torture us, but at least you gave us quite the treat first with this hot number that had my pulse racing!!<br /><br />I was so excited to get my hands on this book when I first read about it, and Leighton seems to get better every time so I was expecting great things. In Down to You, Olivia is just your average girl with the typical financial woes that college students go through. Moving in with her pretentious, overbearing cousin was not what she'd ever choose if it weren't the last resort. And when she meets her cousin's gorgeous boyfriend and can't help but notice the intense sparks between them, after sharing a near-steamy moment with his twin brother the night before, Olivia knows she's in for it. Thus begins the tumultuous bad-boy vs. good-boy whirlwind, and it was a truly dizzying ride! Leighton did a phenomenal job at giving both Cash and Nash qualities that you can't help but swoon and lust after, often blurrying the line between one and the other with moments that had me panting and fanning myself! Honestly, Leighton outdid herself with this one, there were so many piping-hot episodes of fiery steaminess that I had to take a break just to catch my breath! IT. WAS. AWESOME!!!! <br /><br /><b> “So that's how you charm the cobra," I quip. He smiles devilishly. "If you really want to see what effect you have on my snake, I'd be happy to show you.” </b><br /><br /><b> “His eyes meet mine and one brow rises in that holy mother of hell-sexy way, then he mutters, "You've got one chance to make my mouth water.” </b><br /><br />As I sat battling with myself through the whole story over who should win out, Cash or Nash, I was banging my head against the wall wondering how in the world Olivia would ever decide. Cash was so much more than just the drop-dead gorgeous bad-boy; I just loved the sexy banter and cute flirtation they had, but he was also such a sweetheart behind all his cocky swagger. And Nash was so much more than the intelligent, romantic dreamboat, at times showing the same sexy confidence that his twin has. It infuriated me to no end that Olivia kept shoving Cash aside in her head as the self-labeled "bad boy who will break my heart", even before we got to see how much more there was to him, but I wrote that off as her past getting in the way. She tried to not give him a chance from the start b/c of her history with men, but I'm so glad Cash pushed his way through her stubborn defenses to show his true colors. I loved both of them, but Cash was the one that really won me over!! <br /><br /><b> “I shouldn't have stayed as long as I did, but I wanted to hold her while she slept. I wanted her to know I wasn't going anywhere. That she was safe with me. In my arms.” </b><br /><br />And I've got to hand it to Leighton, I was SO not expecting the HUGE bomb that Cash drops on Olivia!! Talk about a shocking, "WTF??!!" revelation that would forever change their lives!! I loved it!!! It solved all my issues with Cash and Nash, and it was such an exciting twist in this great story! I flew through this book b/c I just couldn't put it down, and holy crap that ending!! I was thinking to myself 'oh, well I guess it's just wrapping up nicely', and then BAM!! I find out that not only is there another book, but Down to You ends with a shocking twist that has my stomach all tied up...please don't let it be a long wait for the sequel, because I can't take it!!!!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="10820911726280864072" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_15981894'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15981894-devoured"><img alt="Devoured (Devoured, #1)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1347063810l/15981894._SX98_.jpg" />

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZM+XmYx253j5ymdlGIfAbnS2h7zuqIBm1bwYSpwfS6Gp+qrbvOz5J+Oz025dYBNj+Epu7LxY1pBNdrhlhCiiEQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('xFIVP/5J4Vs0kmNn/LiE0W6w15aoG5I6s8teClBW55QJZyh9ztP/BC7r12y5X1fc4kw+xvrrxMwrAf4lSGEOJA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer6585613112301962091">New York Times and USA Today Bestselling Author, M. Leighton, is a native of Ohio. She relocated to the warmer climates of the South, where she can be near the water all summer and miss the snow all winter. Possessed of an overactive imagination from early in her childhood, Michelle finally found an acceptable outlet for her fantastical visions: literary fiction. Having written over a dozen novels</span>
  <span id="freeText6585613112301962091" style="display:none">New York Times and USA Today Bestselling Author, M. Leighton, is a native of Ohio. She relocated to the warmer climates of the South, where she can be near the water all summer and miss the snow all winter. Possessed of an overactive imagination from early in her childhood, Michelle finally found an acceptable outlet for her fantastical visions: literary fiction. Having written over a dozen novels, these days Michelle enjoys letting her mind wander to more romantic settings with sexy Southern guys, much like the one she married and the ones you'll find in her latest books. When her thoughts aren't roaming in that direction, she'll be riding wild horses, skiing the slopes of Aspen or scuba diving with a hot rock star, all without leaving the cozy comfort of her office.<br /><br />About Michelle: I love coffee and chocolate, even more so when they are combined. I'm convinced that one day they could be the basis for world peace. I also love the color red and am seriously considering dying my hair.<br /></span>
